font-size: large;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 225.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 225.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-size: x-large;\">Type I</span></span></b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-size: x-large;\"> ships</span> must be able to survive assumed damage anywhere in their length. Cargo tanks for the most dangerous products should be located outside the extent of the assumed damage and at least 760mm from the ship's shell.&nbsp; </span></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 225.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 225.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\"><span style=\"background-color: yellow;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">IMO type&nbsp;1, 2 and 3</span>. Other cargoes, which present a lesser hazard may be carried in tanks next to the hull-&nbsp; ( incl diluted slops after tank washings )&nbsp; See layout below--</span></span></span></span></span><br />\n</div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-BHJe35sH6bw/TnjNQkD9PUI/AAAAAAAAGTk/KiNKZzY4y4o/s1600/Jo+Eik+Layout.gif\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"152\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-BHJe35sH6bw/TnjNQkD9PUI/AAAAAAAAGTk/KiNKZzY4y4o/s400/Jo+Eik+Layout.gif\" width=\"400\" /></a></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: large;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 225.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">Some of the chemicals carried on type one ships are Chlorosulphonic acid, Dodecyl phenol, Phosphorous yellow/ white, Tricresyl Phosphate (&gt;1% ortho-isomer), Trixylyl Phosphate.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: large;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 225.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">Maximum tank size is 1250 M3. <o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: large;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 225.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">Double side width B/5 or 11.5 mtrs which ever is less.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: large;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 225.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">DB depth B/15 or 6 mtrs at centre line, but not &lt; 760mm .<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: large;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 225.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">Auto ignition temperature of cargoes &lt;65 deg C.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: large;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 225.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">Explosive range &gt;50% by volume in air.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: large;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 225.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">Type 1 offers highest limit of containment.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: large;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 225.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: large;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: large;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: large;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 225.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-size: x-large;\">Type II</span></span></b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-size: x-large;\"> ships</span>, if more than 150m in length, must be able to survive assumed damage anywhere in their length; if less than 150m, the ship should survive assumed damage anywhere except when it involves either of the bulkheads bounding machinery spaces located aft. Tanks for Type II cargoes should be located at least 760mm from the ship's shell and outside the extent of assumed grounding damage.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: large;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 225.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">Maximum tank size is 3000 M3.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: large;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 225.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">Capable of stripping tanks &lt;100 litres.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: large;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 225.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">Auto ignition temp of cargoes &lt;200 deg C.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: large;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 225.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">Explosive range &gt;40% by volume in air.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: large;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 225.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: large;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 225.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-size: x-large;\">Type III</span></span></b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-size: x-large;\"> ships</span>, if more than 125m in length, should be capable of surviving assumed damage anywhere in their length except when it involves either of the bulkheads bounding the machinery space.&nbsp; If less than 125m in length, they should be capable of surviving damage anywhere unless it involves machinery spaces. There is no special requirement for cargo tank location. No limit for size of tank.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: large;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; tab-stops: 225.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">Capable of stripping tanks &lt;300 litres with tolerance of 50 litres.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: large;\">  </span><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: large;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: #231f20; No money or expensive infrastructure is required.<br />\n<br />\nMy favourite running scene for a long time was in one of the Jerry Springer&nbsp;shows, where&nbsp;a obese man mountain was told \" If you run from here to there in 10 seconds, this juicy triple combo beef sandwich is yours \".<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-z1zNa7tqzSs/TncJhyIiNWI/AAAAAAAAGQI/IL_Tqh0CQxA/s1600/imagesCA55X6ZH.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-z1zNa7tqzSs/TncJhyIiNWI/AAAAAAAAGQI/IL_Tqh0CQxA/s1600/imagesCA55X6ZH.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nAnd the fat man just did it.&nbsp; He ran like the whirling dervish, as if there was no tomorrow. <br />\n<br />\nShows what magic incentives can do.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-XjmWTROAZ3Y/TncJ4u4Hw4I/AAAAAAAAGQM/U6ZkEWUYo-s/s1600/SER.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-XjmWTROAZ3Y/TncJ4u4Hw4I/AAAAAAAAGQM/U6ZkEWUYo-s/s1600/SER.JPG\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nGoes to show how much motivation can do to move lard mountains.<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-LaQKTRhKI-8/TncKLTZA4_I/AAAAAAAAGQU/ImIEB3iZ1Q4/s1600/imagesCA36RGY5.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-LaQKTRhKI-8/TncKLTZA4_I/AAAAAAAAGQU/ImIEB3iZ1Q4/s1600/imagesCA36RGY5.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThen came along the Hollywood movie Forrest Gump acted out by Tom Hanks-- tailor made for him. It is about a simpleton with a low IQ of 75 from Alabama, with a speech impediment. <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-f0DksbZfmRQ/TncKFPGSHDI/AAAAAAAAGQQ/uySyCn6qP64/s1600/VCX.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-f0DksbZfmRQ/TncKFPGSHDI/AAAAAAAAGQQ/uySyCn6qP64/s1600/VCX.png\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nHis love Jenny sleeps with him for a night and leaves the next morning&nbsp;. She did not respond to his marriage proposal , but tells him that she loves him, and leaves it at that. . <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-uNvbTvUeKNI/TngP_yk-9UI/AAAAAAAAGTM/TB0otGUA-Go/s1600/bdw.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-uNvbTvUeKNI/TngP_yk-9UI/AAAAAAAAGTM/TB0otGUA-Go/s1600/bdw.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nIn his hour of extreme personal distress , simpleton Forrest Gump remembers what his dead mama had told him<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">.\" You got to put the past behind you before you can move on!\".</span> <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-dzSDE4HZ9Ws/TngQGDhfjKI/AAAAAAAAGTQ/-WFklitbLQw/s1600/xcb.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-dzSDE4HZ9Ws/TngQGDhfjKI/AAAAAAAAGTQ/-WFklitbLQw/s1600/xcb.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nUnable to come in terms with the loss of the love of his life Jenny, the deaths of his&nbsp;mama and his bosom buddy Bubba,&nbsp; and to avoid sinking into acute depression -- he decided to do just what his dear mama had told him-- leave things behind. <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-RDmldyg4tuw/TngQM0_ehLI/AAAAAAAAGTU/itnLjndB2gY/s1600/images+%252812%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-RDmldyg4tuw/TngQM0_ehLI/AAAAAAAAGTU/itnLjndB2gY/s1600/images+%252812%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\nHe goes for a run. <br />\n<br />\nAnd then he decides not to stop. <br />\n<br />\n<br />\nFor the next 3 years, 2 months , 14 days and 17 hours Forrest Gumps nay runs&nbsp;across USA. <br />\n<br />\nContrary to the proverb&nbsp;\" a&nbsp;rolling stone gathers no moss\" , he develops a small following who are happy to just run along behind&nbsp;him. <br />\n<br />\nHe runs hard , troubled and hounded by old memories-- of how he ran from bullies to escape a beating, how he ran in Vietnam to save a comrade in arms , and how Jenny ignored him, and his sad life without mama. . <br />\n<br />\nOne day he gets to terms with himself , he snaps out of it and suddenly stops , with a bunch of confused and bewildered followers behind him. <br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-size: large;\">What to do next?!</span>&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\nA young guy behind him silences the crowd buzz and cries \" Quiet, he's gonna say somethin' !\" <br />\n<br />\nForrest Gump says softly \" I'm pretty tired now, I think I will go home now!\". <br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\nThis scenic spot on the highway&nbsp;between Mexican Hat and Monument Valley Utah where Forrest Gump stopped running , and jacked all his followers, is now a famous tourist spot. <br />\n<br />\nThis is how much impact this unique long run in a low budget Hollywood movie , had on everybody on this planet.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; This is what&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red; font-size: x-large;\">TRAILBLAZING</span> is all about- ok?.<br />\n<br />\nAnd then along comes, <span style=\"color: blue; font-size: x-large;\">&nbsp;THE character</span>-- Jamaican Usain Bolt , who gave us all on this planet&nbsp;, our greatest moment of sporting history. Yes, the Beijing Olympics, where he set a world record in the 100 metres dash- &nbsp;nay- bolt.<br />\n<br />\nUsain Bolt was born to run. He exemplifies the joy of running. <br />\n<br />\nHere was a natural showman who celebrated before a race. He was not cocky, he was just himself.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://1.gvt0.com/vi/qslbf8L9nl0/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/qslbf8L9nl0&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/qslbf8L9nl0&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\nAt the finish , he was so far ahead of the bunch, he stops sprinting the&nbsp;last 20 metres and just flows along the river, thumping his chest with his arms widely stretched in celebratory mode .<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">THE DENIZENS OF THE ENTIRE PLANET JUST BLEW THEIR COLLECTIVE MINDS.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-UbYdLk0QV7w/TncKomS3raI/AAAAAAAAGQc/RgoA8B4NVLU/s1600/imagesCA9WWN7T.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-UbYdLk0QV7w/TncKomS3raI/AAAAAAAAGQc/RgoA8B4NVLU/s1600/imagesCA9WWN7T.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nHe pulverised his own world record of 9.72 seconds and set a new one of 9.69 seconds.&nbsp; He made the whole dang thing look so simple. He was so laid back at the start of the race , that he ran with untied shoe laces. <br />\n<br />\nExperts opine, after computer inputs , that he could had clocked 9.51 seconds and set a world record which could have never been broken for centuries-- had he taken the race seriously. <br />\n<br />\nHe then went ahead and broke his own world record&nbsp;at Berlin clocking 9.58 seconds, this time without horsing around, setting all speculations that he is NOT YET a phenomenon, &nbsp;to permanent rest..<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-BQ92GaQMnj8/TncKs0p283I/AAAAAAAAGQg/65awkAP_ICI/s1600/imagesCA6RTD0K.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-BQ92GaQMnj8/TncKs0p283I/AAAAAAAAGQg/65awkAP_ICI/s1600/imagesCA6RTD0K.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\nAbove picture shows our BIG cheetah, with a TINY cheetah!<br />\n<br />\nImmediately his uppity detractors including IOC president Jacques Rogge, condemned Bolt and wanted to blackball him and strip him off the gold medal , for showing disrespect. <br />\n<br />\nThey had done it in the past for the infamous\" black power salute\",&nbsp;-- to John Carlos and Tommy Smith ( he smashed the world record in this 200&nbsp;metres event ) in the 1968 Mexico Olympics.&nbsp; They were on familiar ground.<br />\n<br />\nThis was just a \" human rights salute\" -- misinterpreted to suit the white man's mood swings.&nbsp; In that era the black man was an full American with full rights and respect only during Olympics-- and that too only the world record holders. A devout and articulate black Catholic man could NOT even be a priest.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-mdkRG4Q2R9Q/TncKzj0GToI/AAAAAAAAGQk/BZIma8VjhC0/s1600/sert.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-mdkRG4Q2R9Q/TncKzj0GToI/AAAAAAAAGQk/BZIma8VjhC0/s1600/sert.JPG\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThe ball was surely moving this ominous way..<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">How dare a mangy black man misbehave in this manner-- only the white Yank like superbrat John McEnroe can be allowed to get away with this type of bad behaviour, right?.</span><br />\n<br />\nThen someone suggested . Usain is now the people's darling. <br />\n<br />\nPeople love this winner's unique antics and Superman pose. The roars of appreciation are still echoing all over the planet. <br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">There will be riots within the stadium. This <span style=\"color: red;\">Olympics will have to be aborted</span> , if you ever make this silly immature mistake, and you might get a public lynching too.</span> <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-gdgBRZOB6l0/TncK_HxXz6I/AAAAAAAAGQo/mDQqdRQXqRc/s1600/imagesCA9242QF.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-gdgBRZOB6l0/TncK_HxXz6I/AAAAAAAAGQo/mDQqdRQXqRc/s1600/imagesCA9242QF.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThe people of this planet will NOT accept such a gross decision inflicted on this living legend.<br />\n<br />\nThis is a star&nbsp;100 metres finals event, the most played&nbsp;sport on this planet. <br />\n<br />\nIt is&nbsp;NOT some bullshit curling ( spare me!), fencing, boat pulling, horse jumping&nbsp;or gymnastics, Western nations have made and introduced to gain easy medals&nbsp;to show a good medal tally and hence racial superiority.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-j2jDuuUJkTA/TncLoAnf4NI/AAAAAAAAGQ8/zkw80Glc56M/s1600/imagesCAPERJW3.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-j2jDuuUJkTA/TncLoAnf4NI/AAAAAAAAGQ8/zkw80Glc56M/s1600/imagesCAPERJW3.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nJamaican minister Edmund Barlett vigorously supported Bolt , switched himself to wisdom mode&nbsp;and opined&nbsp;tersely&nbsp;<span style=\"color: blue;\">\" The celebrations are appropriate. You have to see the glory of dem moment!\"</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-UhRzCV7rBIA/TncLHdhm-UI/AAAAAAAAGQs/EbtvPidU67o/s1600/imagesCAHN6T5B.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-UhRzCV7rBIA/TncLHdhm-UI/AAAAAAAAGQs/EbtvPidU67o/s1600/imagesCAHN6T5B.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nIf you watch the video, you will notice that the commentary provided by a yank was excellent. A pommie could have never done justice to this truly EPIC&nbsp;lightning Bolt moment of undiluted madness. <br />\n<br />\nNobody dared blink or breathe for 12 seconds. Till 40 metres Usain Bolt was NOT even in the lead, as he is a poor starter off the blocks.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-IflwOarsBz8/TncLSqje7bI/AAAAAAAAGQw/EnX7aCRuaD4/s1600/imagesCACZ6IQ9.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-IflwOarsBz8/TncLSqje7bI/AAAAAAAAGQw/EnX7aCRuaD4/s1600/imagesCACZ6IQ9.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">Can there ever be another delightfully insane moment in sporting history like this?</span><br />\n<br />\nJealous Carl Lewis frothed from his mouth and bitched. font-size: x-large;\">This is also for all major credit card companies to take note.</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-size: x-large;\">Yatra dot com has been cheating several people by using the mobile telephone.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/--wuy-IMJd1Q/Tncf4D8nnkI/AAAAAAAAGRo/r8qGRr-Ufl4/s1600/imagesCAAHLC2C.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/--wuy-IMJd1Q/Tncf4D8nnkI/AAAAAAAAGRo/r8qGRr-Ufl4/s1600/imagesCAAHLC2C.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nYou will get a call , with lot of background noise , from a person who speaks good English--introducing himself as an employee of YATRA DOT COM. <br />\n<br />\nHe will start of by saying that this conversation is being recorded for a training programme.<br />\n<br />\nHe will tell you that you are one of their good customers , as you have given them good business and that they want to present you with their free branded watch costing 3500 rupees.<br />\n<br />\nThen he will want your home address, to send the courier package to-- <br />\n<br />\n-- there is a method to all what follows . <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-62z1IGggs60/Tncf-d9N4PI/AAAAAAAAGRs/1NG2Gp57mn8/s1600/imagesCAMUGWN4.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-62z1IGggs60/Tncf-d9N4PI/AAAAAAAAGRs/1NG2Gp57mn8/s1600/imagesCAMUGWN4.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nHe will keep making mistakes in writing down your address, and get many YES responses from you, as an answer to \" Is this correct? \"<br />\n<br />\nThen he will say he has to verify that this address is the same as the person who gave them such good business. He will ask for your credit card number, all the while telling you not to reveal the 3 digit pin code or the password. He will keep assuring you, that no cheating will be done, as this is just to verify that they are speaking to the right person , to send their yatra dot com branded watch<br />\n<br />\nYou will wonder what is the harm in giving this, as your credit card is still secure. You pay usual bills by writing the credit card number-- even mobile phone bills<br />\n<br />\nHe will also want to know the expiry date of the card and the Bank which issued it .<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-fZ4fmjiHT0M/TncgFHi6JyI/AAAAAAAAGRw/8ZGwrwvxhN8/s1600/imagesCAHXAIU4.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-fZ4fmjiHT0M/TncgFHi6JyI/AAAAAAAAGRw/8ZGwrwvxhN8/s1600/imagesCAHXAIU4.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThen he will say that he have certain schemes for you , and then he will rattle off at least two dozen schemes -- which cannot be heard clearly over the back ground noise --like in a huge canteen . It cannot be a call centre as they don't give this type of human voice clutter. This schemes will be about discounts to shopping vouchers, international and domestic travel, holiday resort stays etc.<br />\n<br />\nThen he will say that his boss will now go through the same procedure--and he will call<span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\"> within two minutes , again.</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-67o4fcSmFfU/TncgMYZKKrI/AAAAAAAAGR0/K5uwW0NsVJA/s1600/untitledCWY.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; font-size: large;\">After some time a SMS message will come to your mobile that a TRANSACTION OF RUPEES 6067 , HAS BEEN DONE USING YOUR CREDIT CARD NUMBER XXXXX AT YATRA DOT COM ELITE PROGRAMME.</span></b><br />\n<br />\nWhen you call up the number from which you got a call from Yatra dot com-- a voice will say that no such number exists.<br />\n<br />\nWhen you realise you have been cheated and call up your credit card company, they will say <span style=\"color: blue;\">--\" THIS IS NORMAL.&nbsp; Oysters , clams and mussels ( Kadukka ) have high levels of sexual performance enhancing zinc and proteins and aid in releasing sexual hormones like testosterone and estrogen. However they have lot of calories, and you need to be non-vegetarian and living next to the sea coast.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ke0ZhWxUHZo/TmtHeQrCCTI/AAAAAAAAGEk/zhD0XES47Fo/s1600/imagesCABZFIFD.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" nba=\"true\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ke0ZhWxUHZo/TmtHeQrCCTI/AAAAAAAAGEk/zhD0XES47Fo/s1600/imagesCABZFIFD.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThere is a cheap vegetable which can do much more. <br />\n<br />\nThis is where Muringa comes in.<br />\n<br />\nMuringakai first developed in Kerala and Sri Lanka. From there it spread to the whole of India as an Ayurvedic herb and food. After the British invaded India it has been planted all around the globe. India is still the largest producer of Moringa on this planet. This plant though tropical, is a survivor and needs little water, but loves the hot sun.<br />\n<br />\nThis fast growing tree can be planted just by shoving a small branch into the ground, the right end down. Make sure you trim the tree regularly , or it grows too tall, and you cant get the leaves and drumsticks. As per 7000 year old written Ayurvedic texts ,the whole tree is useful, including its fruit, leaves, flowers bark, sap and roots. In Kerala we have been eating Muringa since the past 1000 years. <br />\n<br />\nIf Popeye the sailor man had heard of Muringa leaves , he would never ever eat spinach. For this leaf does several times more good, and more important it will give him a rock-hard hard-on, which stays longer. <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-yZDUm3lav6k/TmtHyKf3dBI/AAAAAAAAGEw/5D1bHsfJ_0Y/s1600/hgf.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" nba=\"true\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-yZDUm3lav6k/TmtHyKf3dBI/AAAAAAAAGEw/5D1bHsfJ_0Y/s1600/hgf.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nIn Kerala the bridegroom is invariable given Avial curry on his wedding night, whose main ingredient is Muringakai , the long vegetable\u2014also known as drumstick. And next day, just inspect his back\u2014it will be scratched and bleeding all over. <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-kOGtNFUezto/TmtIRsGPIcI/AAAAAAAAGE0/CJBA_TzrKzI/s1600/imagesCAN4O46N.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" nba=\"true\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-kOGtNFUezto/TmtIRsGPIcI/AAAAAAAAGE0/CJBA_TzrKzI/s1600/imagesCAN4O46N.jpg\" /></a></div>\nOn the next day after my wedding , we had to go to a local temple. There I had to remove my shirt , as is tradition and men and women stand in different lines. I was wondering why all girls were giggling and having a ball, while my wife alone was standing there red faced and grim with a wrinkle on her chin. (<span style=\"color: blue;\"><em> I hope my wife does NOT read this , for she will kick mE ass</em></span> )<br />\n<br />\nSambhar curry for the Tamils has Muringa as a major ingredient.<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-NIOXCTK5yOY/TmtG7ZuRn5I/AAAAAAAAGEQ/fynBY_0Vfnk/s1600/export2-250x250.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" nba=\"true\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-NIOXCTK5yOY/TmtG7ZuRn5I/AAAAAAAAGEQ/fynBY_0Vfnk/s1600/export2-250x250.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nGram for gram powerhouse Muringa leaves have more Iron than spinach, Calcium than milk ( 3 times ) , Potassium than bananas ( 2 times ) , vitamin C than oranges ( 6 times ) , Vitamin A than carrots ( 4 times ) and rivals protein from eggs without the cholesterol from yellow yolk..<br />\n<br />\nNever mind what others say, Muringa is best when fresh. It loses a percentage of its properties when dried and powdered. WHO recommends Muringa in daily diet, and I am sure they know what they say.<br />\n<br />\nNeed I say more? It is one of the&nbsp;oldest festivals of India. The cultural heritage of Kerala comes into full bloom at this time.<br />\n<br />\nKing Mahabali ruled Kerala in 12000 BC. He was a very just , generous and righteous ruler. There was no crime or greed or jealousy. There was goodness and prosperity everywhere, and people did not even tell a lie. <br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-EAAGqnjwjzM/TmoPvKbmdbI/AAAAAAAAGCg/8ae2XidgQvc/s1600/untitledasd.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" nba=\"true\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-EAAGqnjwjzM/TmoPvKbmdbI/AAAAAAAAGCg/8ae2XidgQvc/s1600/untitledasd.png\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThe people were so happy in his Kingdom that they stopped worshipping the gods . One day King Mahabali decided to do the Ashwamedha yagna. &nbsp;Usually by doing this a king seeks to secure his authority as an emperor and dares any nearby king to challenge his authority bu sending a horse into his kingdom.<br />\n<br />\nThose days all gods belonged to one sect called Devas, while King Mahabali ( or Maveli ) belonged to the Asura sect.<br />\n<br />\nThis made the King of Gods , Indra very jealous and nervous. He prevailed on Aditi, his mother to convince Vishnu to correct this imbalance. Vishnu decided to intervene and took the avatar of Vamana --a blue faced Brahmin midget ( dwarf ) .<br />\n<br />\nAfter this avatar Vishnu, came later as Parashurama, Rama , Krishna ( 4000 BC ) &nbsp;and Ayyappa&nbsp; . <br />\n<br />\nOn Dec 21st 2012 Vishnu's last and 10th avatar will be Kalki, on a white horse.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Ud_XvhxJs2I/TmpJzp8GP1I/AAAAAAAAGD4/LEu5-aeqZ8U/s1600/imagesCA996BG1.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" nba=\"true\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Ud_XvhxJs2I/TmpJzp8GP1I/AAAAAAAAGD4/LEu5-aeqZ8U/s320/imagesCA996BG1.jpg\" width=\"249\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-1FYGHdjM4KM/TmoQZA-qRsI/AAAAAAAAGC4/5UF_U5xcyq4/s1600/PLG.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" nba=\"true\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-1FYGHdjM4KM/TmoQZA-qRsI/AAAAAAAAGC4/5UF_U5xcyq4/s400/PLG.jpg\" width=\"330\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThe Brahmin dwarf asked King Mahabali for alms-- a small grant of land.&nbsp; The King told him that he can take as much land area as he wished, within his kingdom . But the midget wanted only three strides ( paces ) &nbsp;of land. <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-0JSsWiW69tI/TmpKB7dFIoI/AAAAAAAAGD8/74axN3qfd8g/s1600/imagesCAYPUCFU.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" nba=\"true\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-0JSsWiW69tI/TmpKB7dFIoI/AAAAAAAAGD8/74axN3qfd8g/s400/imagesCAYPUCFU.jpg\" width=\"299\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nImmediately the kings advisor Sage Shukracharya who was a seer, advised his king NOT to agree to this request, as he suspected something amiss and was sure of foul play. <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-R0AVPE5tH4c/TmoZjK6DYgI/AAAAAAAAGDc/CPF4YkBZe8c/s1600/kalari%252B1.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" nba=\"true\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-R0AVPE5tH4c/TmoZjK6DYgI/AAAAAAAAGDc/CPF4YkBZe8c/s400/kalari%252B1.jpg\" width=\"268\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nMahabali being a very&nbsp;generous king, could NOT imagine going back on his word, during a divine sacrifice. <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/--IL_-jZy7gs/TmpJRkcLYII/AAAAAAAAGDk/93C9yVXF69k/s1600/bdw.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" nba=\"true\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/--IL_-jZy7gs/TmpJRkcLYII/AAAAAAAAGDk/93C9yVXF69k/s320/bdw.png\" width=\"261\" /></a></div>\nSo he agreed to grant the boon of three paces of land.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\nVamana then assumed the gigantic form of Vishnu ( the Preserver lord ) and in the first two steps covered the whole of earth and cosmos. <br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-oSK07a_itB0/TmpJWG1OhtI/AAAAAAAAGDo/VFKTGY-MWaA/s1600/imagesCAKLTV28.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" nba=\"true\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-oSK07a_itB0/TmpJWG1OhtI/AAAAAAAAGDo/VFKTGY-MWaA/s640/imagesCAKLTV28.jpg\" width=\"379\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThen he asked the king where he should keep his third step. The king bowed down on his knees and told him to place the third step on his head. <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-6Uvl5LA-Shw/TmpJakH4RdI/AAAAAAAAGDs/XlnqINwL7Fs/s1600/imagesCAUMS81C.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" nba=\"true\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-6Uvl5LA-Shw/TmpJakH4RdI/AAAAAAAAGDs/XlnqINwL7Fs/s320/imagesCAUMS81C.jpg\" width=\"272\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nBefore that he asked that he should be able to visit and bless his subjects&nbsp;once every year . <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-GNRHryivB5M/TmpJhkoprlI/AAAAAAAAGDw/xfGGG9g6pNk/s1600/untitled.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" nba=\"true\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-GNRHryivB5M/TmpJhkoprlI/AAAAAAAAGDw/xfGGG9g6pNk/s320/untitled.png\" width=\"203\" /></a></div>\nVishnu granted this boon and placed his foot on Mahabali's head and instead of driving him underground to the netherworld , he sent him to heaven -- pleased with his righteousness.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-57ZSxkpr2h4/TmpJm41_9rI/AAAAAAAAGD0/qiuE6oJGOY0/s1600/untitledbd.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" nba=\"true\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-57ZSxkpr2h4/TmpJm41_9rI/AAAAAAAAGD0/qiuE6oJGOY0/s320/untitledbd.png\" width=\"194\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-tDyY9gZevzw/TmoP7Kv-t6I/AAAAAAAAGCo/Ayw6VT8MWUo/s1600/imagesCA08SG7K.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"302\" nba=\"true\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-tDyY9gZevzw/TmoP7Kv-t6I/AAAAAAAAGCo/Ayw6VT8MWUo/s320/imagesCA08SG7K.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red;\">THIS IS THE REASON WHY ALL MALAYALIS CELEBRATE ONAM -- THE DAY THE KING WILL COME EVERY YEAR. &nbsp;A CARPET OF FRESH FLOWERS IS LAID AT THE ENTRANCE OF EVERY HOUSE.&nbsp; THIS HARVEST SEASON FESTIVAL IS SECULAR AND IT SYMBOLISES THE ADVAITHA PRINCIPLE.</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: blue;\">DIWALI OR DEEPAWALI MARKS THE VICTORY OF GODS , OR DEFEAT OF KING MAHABALI .&nbsp; </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: blue;\">DIWALI IS CELEBRATED BY THE WHOLE OF INDIA-- EXCEPT KERALA</span>.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-PITmbQ3VV8k/TmoQPeSe_fI/AAAAAAAAGC0/T4t13MAfNns/s1600/imagesCAPJ27TS.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" nba=\"true\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-PITmbQ3VV8k/TmoQPeSe_fI/AAAAAAAAGC0/T4t13MAfNns/s400/imagesCAPJ27TS.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\nOn Onam day everybody has a holiday and he feasts ( traditional vegetarian cuisine&nbsp;) on a banana leaf, like in the good old days . All wear new clothes . The ancient dessert of sweet payasam is enjoyed. The festivities go on for a full 10 days and it culminates with Thiruvonam .<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-hHipTUc6jCc/TmoQK7zqLdI/AAAAAAAAGCw/nUHFQD3du98/s1600/TDA.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"300\" nba=\"true\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-hHipTUc6jCc/TmoQK7zqLdI/AAAAAAAAGCw/nUHFQD3du98/s400/TDA.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nSince Mahabali, this fabled land of Kerala always had the most advanced society of India. The people are highly aware and the culture is very deep rooted. When the whole of India burns due to intolerance, Kerala is an oasis of peace. <br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-2od75Smg9BA/TmoZdJ0Cc6I/AAAAAAAAGDY/JXVZepSb59k/s1600/festival.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" nba=\"true\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-2od75Smg9BA/TmoZdJ0Cc6I/AAAAAAAAGDY/JXVZepSb59k/s400/festival.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThis state has produced very eminent rishis and Maharishis. After the river Saraswati dried up in 4000 BC, there was an exodus down south to Kerala. A lot of the migrants settled down at the river Zuari ( Goa till the Portuguese started their inquisition ). This was NOT an Indian Aryan invasion--they were given refuge by Dravidians.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-mEJSMITbmLI/TmoZY5gC3BI/AAAAAAAAGDU/UMpprkSQ6r8/s1600/chenda.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" nba=\"true\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-mEJSMITbmLI/TmoZY5gC3BI/AAAAAAAAGDU/UMpprkSQ6r8/s400/chenda.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nMaha means great and Bali means sacrifice --both in Malayalam and in Sanskrit. Mahabali's grandfather was Prahalad whose father Hiranyakashyap was slain by Vishnu in his Narasimha avatar ( before Vamana avatar ).<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-uM5tVvhR0I4/TmoQiRxV7JI/AAAAAAAAGC8/4JXJNk0bm3A/s1600/imagesCAT9N2N8.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"237\" nba=\"true\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-uM5tVvhR0I4/TmoQiRxV7JI/AAAAAAAAGC8/4JXJNk0bm3A/s400/imagesCAT9N2N8.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"color: black;\">Every Malayali even if he works abroad, Christian or Muslim-- knows this 8000 year old Malayalam song-- if he does NOT , he is only a pseudo Malayali. </span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"color: black;\">Onam is Kerala's most important cultural festival -- to remind the denizens of a once blissful, harmonious and happy era--under the rule of a benevolent king..</span></span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-GbaUDpapRlU/TmoV5U8IhbI/AAAAAAAAGDM/cjtZtZJUt3w/s1600/stl.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" nba=\"true\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-GbaUDpapRlU/TmoV5U8IhbI/AAAAAAAAGDM/cjtZtZJUt3w/s1600/stl.png\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><em>maveli nadu vaneedum kalam,<br />\nmanusharellarum onnupole<br />\namodhathode vasikkum kalam<br />\napathangarkkumottillathanum<br />\nkallavum illa chathiyumilla<br />\nellolamilla polivachanam<br />\nkallapparayum cherunazhiyum<br />\nkallatharangal mattonnumilla<br />\nadhikal vyadhikalonnumilla<br />\nbalamaranangal kelppanilla</em></span><br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">When Maveli our king ruled the land </span></i></div>\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">All the people were equal.<br />\nAnd people were joyful and merry;<br />\nThey were all free from harm.<br />\nThere was neither anxiety nor sickness,<br />\nDeaths of children were unheard of,<br />\nThere were no lies,<br />\nThere was neither theft nor deceit,<br />\nAnd no one was false in speech either.<br />\nMeasures and weights were right;<br />\nNo one cheated or wronged his neighbor.<br />\nWhen Maveli, our King, ruled the land,<br />\nAll the people formed one caste less race</span></i><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-YZQGgwW7z6M/TmoVqMv-_WI/AAAAAAAAGDI/uzY1i9fLUMs/s1600/untitledfgd.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" nba=\"true\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-YZQGgwW7z6M/TmoVqMv-_WI/AAAAAAAAGDI/uzY1i9fLUMs/s1600/untitledfgd.png\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nVishnu came in his next Avatar as warrior sage Lord Parashurama. After Mahabali left Kerala , the land was oppressed by the Kshatriya ruling class. <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-u9ElRsv_yLo/TmpJDMURd4I/AAAAAAAAGDg/9BThD3FL8zw/s1600/images%252B%2525286%252529%25281%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" nba=\"true\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-u9ElRsv_yLo/TmpJDMURd4I/AAAAAAAAGDg/9BThD3FL8zw/s1600/images%252B%2525286%252529%25281%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\nParashurama's ( Ram with an axe ) mission was to destroy the oppressing Kshatriyas. He threw his axe northwards&nbsp;along the coast line from Kanyakumari and reclaimed land from the sea, as per lore.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-BGxG4FfTe8M/TmoVeZkXTgI/AAAAAAAAGDA/_Ae1de5RVBI/s1600/imagesCA7CRZNT.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" nba=\"true\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-BGxG4FfTe8M/TmoVeZkXTgI/AAAAAAAAGDA/_Ae1de5RVBI/s1600/imagesCA7CRZNT.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nA lot on my childhood memories are attached to the Onam festivities when we as a bunch of happy kids went to pluck flowers , mainly Thumbapoo and Chemabrithipoo. Nowadays children tell their parents to pay money and buy flowers from the market. <br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-cf85lR_NIhs/TmoVh6u9lbI/AAAAAAAAGDE/3F41R32c3LA/s1600/imagesCA5A2SIR.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" nba=\"true\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-cf85lR_NIhs/TmoVh6u9lbI/AAAAAAAAGDE/3F41R32c3LA/s1600/imagesCA5A2SIR.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThe joy was in collecting the flowers, and the competition and adventure attached to it , by climbing trees , crossing streams etc.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-gmz-yoT2HAI/TmoZTRtufrI/AAAAAAAAGDQ/f3Lt9sipROQ/s1600/images%252B%2525289%252529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" nba=\"true\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-gmz-yoT2HAI/TmoZTRtufrI/AAAAAAAAGDQ/f3Lt9sipROQ/s1600/images%252B%2525289%252529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; Lord Shiva killed Banasura the evil son of King Mahabali .<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"avatar-image-container\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; float: left; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; So I was given one, whose handwriting was excellent.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Ny64A7Alwng/TmX6ZRP_6ZI/AAAAAAAAGBc/LLVZUphb90c/s1600/imagesCAQLBVJ2.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Ny64A7Alwng/TmX6ZRP_6ZI/AAAAAAAAGBc/LLVZUphb90c/s1600/imagesCAQLBVJ2.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nIn between the guy ( or was it a gal? - let it be !) told me that he wanted to be a doctor . My knee jerk reaction was to tell him \" OK, then very soon your writing is gonna be horrible -- so write well when you have this chance , for posterity!\"<br />\n<br />\nMuch later in life I have seen some medical prescriptions which this yester-year assistant of mine, made as a respected senior doctor. IT WAS AN ILLEGIBLE CHICKEN SCRATCH-- not surprising at all!<br />\n<br />\nSo why do the doctor's make their handwriting deliberately bad? Only their prescriptions are illegible, rest everything else they write , are absolutely legible and clear.<br />\n<br />\nLet me make a statement here-- THE DOCTORS PRESCRIPTION IS THE FRUIT OF HIS FEW MINUTES EXAMINING YOU. IF THIS FRUIT IS NO GOOD, YOU ARE NOT IN THE SAFE ZONE.<br />\n<br />\nNow let me digress--<br />\n<br />\n26 years ago, my ship was at sea and I was asleep. My wife shook me awake at 2 AM. \" Get up, somebody is literally hammering our door. I can hear lot of voices too.\"<br />\n<br />\nI immediately got up , put on my robe and opened the office door. My apartment had 4 rooms, a pantry and a washroom, being a huge Swedish Built tanker.<br />\n<br />\nWhat I saw stunned me-- I could see almost the entire ship's complement in my alleyway-- about 55 of them, -- all looking frightened&nbsp;.<br />\n<br />\nThen my attention shifted to some movement on the floor, and I saw a sailor writhing in pain , rolling around .<br />\n<br />\nImmediately I asked the Bosun \" What is wrong with him?\" <br />\n<br />\nThe Bosun said \" I don't know, but he is in great pain !\"<br />\n<br />\nThen I asked \" Who is is cabin mate ?\"<br />\n<br />\nA sailor stepped forward. I asked him the same question.<br />\n<br />\nHe also said he does NOT know. So I asked him to think back, of any unusual conversation during the day.&nbsp; He said \" Yes, he&nbsp;told me while having morning tea that&nbsp;he took too long time to pass&nbsp;the usual routine urine \"<br />\n<br />\nImmediately I came to me bed room and told my wife, to go to Chief Engineers cabin. Then I scooped the writhing sailor on the floor, in my hands and placed him in my bath tub, and removed his pants. <br />\n<br />\nThis was a huge tub , meant for 150 kilo Scandinavian giants , and myself and my wife used to take bath together, those days.<br />\n<br />\nI opened the hot water to keep his waist below water level, and told him to relax and piss into the tub when he is ready. By the time I finished telling him, I could see a yellow trickle gushing out from his prick.<br />\n<br />\nSeeing him smiling , I asked him \" Is there any more pain?\"<br />\n<br />\nHe said \" All pain has disappeared \" &nbsp;.<br />\n<br />\nSo I scooped him in my arms, nude, alongwith his pyjamas -- and took him to my door and slid him on the floor and said \" All of you, FO, back to sleep, don't come back again!\". <br />\n<br />\nThis happy but embarrassed sailor was immediately trying to puts his pyjamas back on, before my wife came back from the Chief Engineers cabin.<br />\n<br />\nYou should have seen the awed faces of my crew.&nbsp; For here was a man about to die in severe pain, -- the Captain takes him in to his room , tells his wife to leave the cabin&nbsp;el pronto, shuts the door, and after 3 minutes opens the door again and slides down nay curls&nbsp;( like the Canadian ice game ) a nude, wet and smiling guy .<br />\n<br />\nLater myself and my wife looked for about 10 minutes , hard by shining a torch trough the yellow water in the white tub, if we can see the small urethra or urinary tract blocking&nbsp;stone, and we saw nothing-- strange! The sailor was OK till he got off the ship after 4 months.<br />\n<br />\nThis is how reputations are earned at sea-- it takes 3 or 4 decades to build a reputation - BUT--&nbsp;you are only as good as your last innings ( unlike Tendulkar ) . Reputations crash in just 3 seconds. One first foot failure or one grounding or one sailor's death --everything carefully built over decades , comes crashing down.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nImagine if this same man was in any place in Kerala, say at 5 PM. His wife makes a call to any doctor, begging him to come fast or alteast give some advise on phone -- what do you think will be the net result-- we all know it.<br />\n<br />\nNow even if his wife takes him to the hospital , what do you think the learned doctor will do?&nbsp; Be frank, doctors!<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-rhLAgxSTnE4/TmX6912IewI/AAAAAAAAGBw/AOC0-xXZP0Q/s1600/imagesCA4AN0LM.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-rhLAgxSTnE4/TmX6912IewI/AAAAAAAAGBw/AOC0-xXZP0Q/s1600/imagesCA4AN0LM.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nLET ME TELL YOU SOMETHING TODAY, THE INTENTION OF THE DOCTOR YOU GO TO IS VERY IMPORTANT. <br />\n<br />\nYou have a severe life and death condition --and the doctor you go to takes his pen and \"chicken scratches\" a prescription which neither you , nor the licenced pharmacist in the Chemists store , is unable to read-- you know how much the doctor cares about you.<br />\n<br />\nThe handwriting of doctors who handle soiled currency notes&nbsp;from poor patients directly , counting it , giving change back and putting the moolah&nbsp;into his table drawer are the worst. The doctors who get a fixed salary from the hospital have slightly better handwriting. <br />\n<br />\nBut BAD handwriting all of them do have.<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-e59zAegAuoY/TmX7D00bg7I/AAAAAAAAGB0/HY4oxhLlF5o/s1600/imagesCA1EUNKQ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-e59zAegAuoY/TmX7D00bg7I/AAAAAAAAGB0/HY4oxhLlF5o/s1600/imagesCA1EUNKQ.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nWhat follows is NOT conjecture--it is an informed opinion. I have consulted hundreds of medical shop ( chemist store ) pharmacists and medical representatives.<br />\n<br />\nMore than 100000 ( one lakh ) patients die due to illegible doctors handwriting every year in India. <br />\n<br />\nAt least 20 lakh patients health is irreversibly damaged due to side effects of overdose or wrong medicines. <br />\n<br />\nWhy does not IMA take note of this shocking state of affairs ?<br />\n<br />\nWhen more than 20000 pharmaceutical generic names and brands are available, why are the doctors so callous. <br />\n<br />\nHave you ever seen a doctor looking into a pharmaceutical pill directory or almanac to check out the actual spelling of the tablets and injection, he prescribes. His ego prevents him from doing so. He wants his patient to think he knows all these thousands of pill&nbsp; generic names.<br />\n<br />\nIF ANY DOCTOR CLAIMS HE KNOWS ALL THE SPELLINGS OF OBSCURE DRUGS , HE CAN BE EASILY CHALLENGED.<br />\n<br />\nNone of these names are taught in Medical college as new names are churned out every day. <br />\n<br />\nMost of the time , the drug store clerk will tell you that that particular brand is NOT available and he will give you a substitute. It is all about making sure drugs don't expire without getting consumed. All play this deadly game.<br />\n<br />\nSome doctors will say that presciptions are made for the pharmacists eyes and hence the patient does NOT need to know. <br />\n<br />\nBULLSHIT! <br />\n<br />\nThis is NOT what your IMA wants. <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-enFn4rHmWCM/TmX6x0FCuOI/AAAAAAAAGBo/GQsP9pxNrqs/s1600/imagesCAJYB44Y.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-enFn4rHmWCM/TmX6x0FCuOI/AAAAAAAAGBo/GQsP9pxNrqs/s1600/imagesCAJYB44Y.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nIf your handwriting is so bad , the why don't you write in capital letters. <br />\n<br />\n<br />\nOR IS IT BECAUSE , IF THE PATIENT DIES, DUE TO WRONG PRESCRIPTION, YOU CANNOT BE PINNED IN A COURT OF LAW?<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-_-9Zg7Mq3jo/TmX6ohAMoaI/AAAAAAAAGBk/vqzrar6T7Q8/s1600/imagesCAP7NA1F.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-_-9Zg7Mq3jo/TmX6ohAMoaI/AAAAAAAAGBk/vqzrar6T7Q8/s1600/imagesCAP7NA1F.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nMost of the time a drug store has one licenced pharmacist. But in Kerala we find his wife, his brother , his kids also chipping in--so that he does NOT have to employ someone and give him a salary. Even if he has employed someone, this soul will not be licenced. What do they know ? You will find them usually peering into the drug almanac to make out head and tail, with a crowd hustling for immediate attention.<br />\n<br />\n<strong><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">WE ALL KNOW THERE IS A HUGE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN HURRIED HANDWRITING AND A DELIBERATE SELF RIGHTEOUS \"CHICKEN SCRATCH\" ,&nbsp;MADE WITH ULTERIOR MOTIVE AND VESTED INTERESTS, TO DISGUISE SOMETHING.</span></strong><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-aDbg-F5mRDA/TmX63dBLB-I/AAAAAAAAGBs/ex4DrIHl5PA/s1600/imagesCA1EUNKQ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-aDbg-F5mRDA/TmX63dBLB-I/AAAAAAAAGBs/ex4DrIHl5PA/s1600/imagesCA1EUNKQ.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThe same doctors will have rock steady hands when making a surgical incision<br />\n<br />\nWhy are doctors who are competent so keen that the patient should remain in the dark about the medicines he consumes?<br />\n<br />\nNote: We are willing to excuse the hassled doctors who handle the OPD departments of accident cases, where a minute delay can cost a life. Or the poor guys who wrote their three hour exams , with dozens of sheets , in the same type of bad handwriting.<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: x-large;\">OR IS THIS ALL ABOUT BULLSHIT \"MEDICAL MYSTIQUE\"?</span> <br />\n<br />\nSorry, ladies and gentlemen , there are too many doctors around -- for this type of mystique.<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-IS4SgKl1SLw/TmX7V2CnZVI/AAAAAAAAGB8/W_kzVaBhSwQ/s1600/LKS.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-IS4SgKl1SLw/TmX7V2CnZVI/AAAAAAAAGB8/W_kzVaBhSwQ/s1600/LKS.png\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThere have been several cases in Mumbai where the pharmacist has been taken to task in court for issuing wrong medicines. Can he make a mistake if the prescription is legible in capital letters.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-dJf96gi7LrI/TmX6hTNAaaI/AAAAAAAAGBg/fAwh2URMGUM/s1600/imagesCARBGDQ4.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em;
